## נֹא (id: 004586000000000)

נֹא
===

נֹא (H4996) — נֹא אָמֹון

name

Names of Locations

No, Thebes \= town, commonly known as Thebes; ◄ located in Egypt; ► center of worship of Amon

[JER 46:25](https://ref.ly/Jer46:25) · [EZK 30:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek30:14) · [EZK 30:15](https://ref.ly/Ezek30:15) · [EZK 30:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek30:16) · [NAM 3:8](https://ref.ly/Nah3:8)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Jeremiah 46:25; Ezekiel 30:14; Ezekiel 30:15; Ezekiel 30:16; Nahum 3:8


## נֹאד (id: 004587000000000)

נֹאד
====

נֹאד (H4997)

noun m

Containers

skin\-bottle \= container ◄ made of a goatskin, the outer side of which has been turned inside; ► used for storing wine or milk

[JOS 9:4](https://ref.ly/Josh9:4) · [JOS 9:13](https://ref.ly/Josh9:13) · [JDG 4:19](https://ref.ly/Judg4:19) · [1SA 16:20](https://ref.ly/1Sam16:20) · [PSA 56:9](https://ref.ly/Ps56:9) · [PSA 119:83](https://ref.ly/Ps119:83)

Sarah Lind

* **Associated Passages:** Joshua 9:4; Joshua 9:13; Judges 4:19; 1 Samuel 16:20; Psalms 56:9; Psalms 119:83


## נאה (id: 004588000000000)

נאה
===

נאה (H4998)

verb · נָאוֶה · נָוֶה

Good \| verb pi

to be beautiful \= state in which humans or parts of their body are considered physically attractive

[SNG 1:10](https://ref.ly/Song1:10)

Right \| verb pi

to be appropriate, to be welcome literally: to be beautiful; hence: \= state in which a certain quality or event is considered appropriate in a particular context

[PSA 93:5](https://ref.ly/Ps93:5) · [ISA 52:7](https://ref.ly/Isa52:7)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Song of Songs 1:10; Psalms 93:5; Isaiah 52:7


## נָאוֶה (id: 004589000000000)

נָאוֶה
======

נָאוֶה (H5000)

adj · נאה

Good

beautiful, lovely \= state in which humans or parts of their body are considered physically attractive

[SNG 1:5](https://ref.ly/Song1:5) · [SNG 2:14](https://ref.ly/Song2:14) · [SNG 4:3](https://ref.ly/Song4:3) · [SNG 6:4](https://ref.ly/Song6:4)

Right

appropriate, fitting, becoming literally: beautiful; hence: \= state in which a certain event is considered appropriate in a particular context

[PSA 33:1](https://ref.ly/Ps33:1) · [PSA 147:1](https://ref.ly/Ps147:1) · [PRO 17:7](https://ref.ly/Prov17:7) · [PRO 19:10](https://ref.ly/Prov19:10) · [PRO 26:1](https://ref.ly/Prov26:1)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Song of Songs 1:5; Song of Songs 2:14; Song of Songs 4:3; Song of Songs 6:4; Psalms 33:1; Psalms 147:1; Proverbs 17:7; Proverbs 19:10; Proverbs 26:1


## נאם (id: 004590000000000)

נאם
===

נאם (H5001)

verb · נְאֻם

Speak \| verb qal

to utter \= action by which humans make a prophetic statement

[JER 23:31](https://ref.ly/Jer23:31)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Jeremiah 23:31


## נְאֻם (id: 004591000000000)

נְאֻם
=====

נְאֻם (H5002)

noun m · נאם

Speak

declaration, utterance \= action by which humans or deities make a prophetic statement; in the case of a deity this is usually done through the mouth of a prophet or seer

## נאף (id: 004592000000000)

נאף
===

נאף (H5003)

verb · נִאוּפִים · נַאֲפוּפִים

Unfaithful \| verb qal, verb pi \| ≈ זנה

to commit adultery \= action by which married humans have voluntary sexual intercourse with other humans who are not their spouse; ≈ often used as a metaphor for treachery or idolatry

## נבל (id: 004622000000000)

נבל
===

נבל (H5034)

verb · נָבָל · נְבָלָה · נַבְלוּת

Dry \| verb qal \| ≈ אבל · אמל · יבשׁ · מלל · מקק · תמם

to wither, to fade \= process by which plants and their products become devoid of moisture, and therefore lose color and bend over ► which may ultimately result in death if circumstances do not change; ≈ associated with drought and destruction, often as punishment from God

[PSA 1:3](https://ref.ly/Ps1:3) · [PSA 37:2](https://ref.ly/Ps37:2) · [ISA 1:30](https://ref.ly/Isa1:30) · [ISA 24:4](https://ref.ly/Isa24:4) · [ISA 24:4](https://ref.ly/Isa24:4) · [ISA 28:1](https://ref.ly/Isa28:1) · [ISA 28:4](https://ref.ly/Isa28:4) · [ISA 34:4](https://ref.ly/Isa34:4) · [ISA 34:4](https://ref.ly/Isa34:4) · [ISA 34:4](https://ref.ly/Isa34:4) · [ISA 40:7](https://ref.ly/Isa40:7) · [ISA 40:8](https://ref.ly/Isa40:8) · [ISA 64:5](https://ref.ly/Isa64:5) · [JER 8:13](https://ref.ly/Jer8:13) · [EZK 47:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek47:12)

Weak \| verb qal

to wear oneself out, to tire oneself out \= process by which humans lose their strength as a result of hard work

[EXO 18:18](https://ref.ly/Exod18:18) · [EXO 18:18](https://ref.ly/Exod18:18)

Afraid \| verb qal

to lose courage, to lose heart \= process by which humans lose courage when confronted with a formidable opponent

[2SA 22:46](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:46) · [PSA 18:46](https://ref.ly/Ps18:46)

Impact

to crumble away \= process by which objects slowly break or fall apart into small pieces

[JOB 14:18](https://ref.ly/Job14:18)

verb · נְבֵלָה

Foolish \| Great

to be foolish \= state in which humans are foolish but think highly of themselves

[PRO 30:32](https://ref.ly/Prov30:32)

Despise \| verb pi \| ≈ נאץ · נטשׁ

to treat with contempt \= action by which humans or deities treat (other) humans, deities or things that belong to God with disrespect

[DEU 32:15](https://ref.ly/Deut32:15) · [JER 14:21](https://ref.ly/Jer14:21) · [MIC 7:6](https://ref.ly/Mic7:6) · [NAM 3:6](https://ref.ly/Nah3:6)

## נגהּ (id: 004635000000000)

נגהּ
====

נגהּ (H5050) — נָגַהּ

verb · נֹגַהּ · נְגֹהֹות

Shine \| verb qal

to shine \= process by which an object gives out or reflects a bright light

[JOB 18:5](https://ref.ly/Job18:5) · [JOB 22:28](https://ref.ly/Job22:28) · [ISA 9:1](https://ref.ly/Isa9:1)

Shine \| verb hif

to cause to shine \= causative process by which someone causes an object to give out or reflect light

[2SA 22:29](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:29) · [PSA 18:29](https://ref.ly/Ps18:29) · [ISA 13:10](https://ref.ly/Isa13:10)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Job 18:5; Job 22:28; Isaiah 9:1; 2 Samuel 22:29; Psalms 18:29; Isaiah 13:10

## נגח (id: 004639000000000)

נגח
===

נגח (H5055)

verb · נַגָּח

Impact \| verb pi, verb qal

to gore \= action by which an animal pierces or stabs humans or other animals with its horns

[EXO 21:28](https://ref.ly/Exod21:28) · [EXO 21:31](https://ref.ly/Exod21:31) · [EXO 21:31](https://ref.ly/Exod21:31) · [EXO 21:32](https://ref.ly/Exod21:32) · [DEU 33:17](https://ref.ly/Deut33:17) · [1KI 22:11](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:11) · [2CH 18:10](https://ref.ly/2Chr18:10) · [EZK 34:21](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:21) · [DAN 8:4](https://ref.ly/Dan8:4)

Impact \| verb pi \| ≈ בוס

to gore, to throw back \= action by which an army causes a severe blow to its enemy, ◄ compared to an animal goring another animal with its horns

[PSA 44:6](https://ref.ly/Ps44:6)

Conflict \| verb hit

to engage in battle literally: to lock horns; hence: \= action by which two armies engage in battle against one another, ◄ like two animals locking horns

[DAN 11:40](https://ref.ly/Dan11:40)

## נֶגַע (id: 004645000000000)

נֶגַע
=====

נֶגַע (H5061)

noun m · נגע

Impact

plague, disease, stroke, wound, assault \= a disease or sickness or wound ◄ caused by another person or sent from God or a deity ► to punish a person or nation for some wrong or disobedience

## נגף (id: 004646000000000)

נגף
===

נגף (H5062)

verb · נֶגֶף · מַגֵּפָה

Impact \| verb qal, verb hit \| ≠ בֶּטַח

**Collocation:** נגף רֶגֶל · נגף רַגְלַיִם

to hurt one's foot (on something) \> to hurt oneself, to stumble \= process by which a human's foot or both feet come in forcible contact with a stone or other object while travelling, ► which may result in stumbling and injury; ≈ usually used in a figurative way to denote sustaining any kind of hardship in life

[PSA 91:12](https://ref.ly/Ps91:12) · [PRO 3:23](https://ref.ly/Prov3:23) · [JER 13:16](https://ref.ly/Jer13:16)

Impact \| verb qal, verb nif

to strike, to strike down, to defeat \= causative action by which humans or animals deliver a heavy blow to other humans or animals, ► resulting in serious harm or injury, and, in the case of an army, defeat

## נֶגֶף (id: 004647000000000)

נֶגֶף

Flow \| verb hif

Dead \| verb hif, verb nif

**Collocation:** נגר עַל־יְדֵי־חֶרֶב

to cause (someone) to die a violent death literally: to pour (people) out on the hands of the sword; hence: \= causative action by which humans or deities cause (other) humans to die a violent death

Move \| verb hif

to pour down stones literally: to pour stones; hence: \= causative action by which deities cause stones to fall down from a higher elevation, ◄ as liquids are poured from a cup

Stance \| verb nif

**Collocation:** נגר יָד

נוח
===

verb · הֲנָחָה · מָנֹוחַ · מְנוּחָה · נוּחַ · נַחַת · נִיחֹחַ · מָנֹוחַ · נֹחַ

Non\-Engage \| verb qal

## נוע (id: 004707000000000)

נוע
===

נוע (H5128)

verb · מְנַעַנְעִים

Move \| verb qal

to move, to sway, to shake \= process by which objects move up and down or sideways

[JDG 9:9](https://ref.ly/Judg9:9) · [JDG 9:11](https://ref.ly/Judg9:11) · [JDG 9:13](https://ref.ly/Judg9:13) · [1SA 1:13](https://ref.ly/1Sam1:13) · [JOB 28:4](https://ref.ly/Job28:4) · [ISA 6:4](https://ref.ly/Isa6:4) · [ISA 7:2](https://ref.ly/Isa7:2)

Move \| verb hif

to move (something), to wag, to shake \= causative process by which humans or supernatural beings cause objects to move up and down or sideways

[2KI 23:18](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:18) · [DAN 10:10](https://ref.ly/Dan10:10) · [AMO 9:9](https://ref.ly/Amos9:9) · [AMO 9:9](https://ref.ly/Amos9:9) · [NAM 3:12](https://ref.ly/Nah3:12)

Move \| verb qal, verb hif

to stray, to wander \= action by which humans move about from place to place without clear destination

[GEN 4:12](https://ref.ly/Gen4:12) · [GEN 4:14](https://ref.ly/Gen4:14) · [PSA 59:16](https://ref.ly/Ps59:16) · [PSA 109:10](https://ref.ly/Ps109:10) · [PSA 109:10](https://ref.ly/Ps109:10) · [LAM 4:14](https://ref.ly/Lam4:14) · [LAM 4:15](https://ref.ly/Lam4:15) · [AMO 4:8](https://ref.ly/Amos4:8) · [AMO 8:12](https://ref.ly/Amos8:12)

Move \| verb hif

to cause to wander \= causative action by which humans or deities cause (other) humans to move about from place to place without clear destination

[NUM 32:13](https://ref.ly/Num32:13) · [2SA 15:20](https://ref.ly/2Sam15:20) · [PSA 59:12](https://ref.ly/Ps59:12)2

Sin \| verb qal

to err, to go astray literally: to wander; hence: \= action by which humans depart from a morally and ethically correct course

[JER 14:10](https://ref.ly/Jer14:10)

Stance \| verb hif

to wag, to shake \= action by which humans move parts of their body up and down or sideways

[2KI 19:21](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:21) · [JOB 16:4](https://ref.ly/Job16:4) · [PSA 22:8](https://ref.ly/Ps22:8) · [PSA 109:25](https://ref.ly/Ps109:25) · [ISA 37:22](https://ref.ly/Isa37:22) · [LAM 2:15](https://ref.ly/Lam2:15) · [ZEP 2:15](https://ref.ly/Zeph2:15)

Unsteady \| verb qal

to tremble literally: to shake; hence: \= process by which humans tremble for fear

[EXO 20:18](https://ref.ly/Exod20:18) · [ISA 7:2](https://ref.ly/Isa7:2) · [ISA 19:1](https://ref.ly/Isa19:1)

Unsteady \| verb qal \| ≈ חגג

to reel, to stagger literally: to sway; hence: \= action by which humans move about in an unsteady way ◄ like someone who is drunk

[PSA 107:27](https://ref.ly/Ps107:27) · [ISA 24:20](https://ref.ly/Isa24:20) · [ISA 24:20](https://ref.ly/Isa24:20) · [ISA 29:9](https://ref.ly/Isa29:9)

Change \| verb qal

to wander, to be uncertain \= process by which a course of action is unsteady and subject to change

[PRO 5:6](https://ref.ly/Prov5:6)

## נוף (id: 004709000000000)

נוף
===

נוף (H5130)

verb · נָפָה · תְּנוּפָה

Sacrifice \| verb hif, verb hof

to wave, to present (an offering) \= action by which humans hold an object in their hands and move it to and fro, ► probably in order to signal to a deity that the object in their hands is intended for them

[EXO 29:24](https://ref.ly/Exod29:24) · [EXO 29:26](https://ref.ly/Exod29:26) · [EXO 29:27](https://ref.ly/Exod29:27) · [EXO 35:22](https://ref.ly/Exod35:22) · [LEV 7:30](https://ref.ly/Lev7:30) · [LEV 8:27](https://ref.ly/Lev8:27) · [LEV 8:29](https://ref.ly/Lev8:29) · [LEV 9:21](https://ref.ly/Lev9:21) · [LEV 10:15](https://ref.ly/Lev10:15) · [LEV 14:12](https://ref.ly/Lev14:12) · [LEV 14:24](https://ref.ly/Lev14:24) · [LEV 23:11](https://ref.ly/Lev23:11) · [LEV 23:11](https://ref.ly/Lev23:11) · [LEV 23:12](https://ref.ly/Lev23:12) · [LEV 23:20](https://ref.ly/Lev23:20) · [NUM 5:25](https://ref.ly/Num5:25) · [NUM 6:20](https://ref.ly/Num6:20) · [NUM 8:11](https://ref.ly/Num8:11) · [NUM 8:13](https://ref.ly/Num8:13) · [NUM 8:15](https://ref.ly/Num8:15) · [NUM 8:21](https://ref.ly/Num8:21)

Hold \| verb hif

to wield, to use (a tool) \= action by which humans hold an implement or tool in their hand and move it up and down for a certain purpose

[EXO 20:25](https://ref.ly/Exod20:25) · [DEU 23:26](https://ref.ly/Deut23:26) · [DEU 27:5](https://ref.ly/Deut27:5) · [JOS 8:31](https://ref.ly/Josh8:31) · [ISA 10:15](https://ref.ly/Isa10:15) · [ISA 10:15](https://ref.ly/Isa10:15)

Non\-Whole \| verb hif

to sieve, to sift literally: to wave; hence: \= causative action by which humans hold a sieve and shake it in order to separate the grain from the remaining chaff and other particles to complete the process of winnowing; ≈ winnowing is often used as a figure of speech to denote the process of distinguishing between good and bad

[ISA 30:28](https://ref.ly/Isa30:28)1

Stance

**Collocation:** הֵנִיף יָד

to wave (one's) hand literally: to wave (one's) hand; hence: \= action by which humans or deities stretch out their arm and move it, ► often as a gesture or signal

verb · נֹפֶת

Scatter \| verb qal

to scatter, to sprinkle \= causative action by which someone takes a quantity of a dry substance or a liquid with one's hand and scatters it over an object

[PRO 7:17](https://ref.ly/Prov7:17)

Scatter \| verb hif

to shower literally: to cause to scatter; hence: \= causative process by which deities cause rain to fall all over an area

[PSA 68:10](https://ref.ly/Ps68:10)

## נוּר (id: 004713000000000)

נוּר
====

נוּר (A5135)

noun c

Fire

fire \= state of burning, in which substances combine chemically with oxygen from the air and give out bright light, heat, and smoke; ► used for cooking, melting, cleansing, heating, and destroying; ≈ many aspects of life are compared with fire, such as anger, jealousy, aggression, wickedness, words, life, certain sicknesses, suffering, etc.

Land \| ≈ חֵלֶק

inheritance, possession, heritage literally: inheritance; hence: \= land as people's personal or communal property, assigned to them by God himself, and to be transferred from one generation to another and to remain within the family or community; ≈ sometimes extended figuratively to refer to Israel as God's own property, and to God as the Levites' property

## נחם (id: 004740000000000)

נחם
===

verb · נֹחַם · נֶחָמָה · נִחֻמִים · תַּנְחוּם · מְנַחֵם · נְחוּם · נַחַם · נְחֶמְיָה · נַחֲמָנִי

Relief \| verb pi, verb hit, verb nif, verb pu'al \| ≈ דבר עַל לֵב · נוד · נשׂא בְּשִׂיח · רחם

to comfort, to console, to reassure, to express sympathy, to bring relief \= causative action by which humans or deities seek to make (other) humans feel relief after a time of grief, anxiety, or fear

to hit, to beat, to strike \= action by which humans deliver a blow to (other) humans, animals, or objects, either with one's bare hands, part of their body, a stick, a whip, or a stone

Impact \| verb hif

**Collocation:** נכה כַּף · נשׁכ בְּכַף

to clap (one's) hands \= action by which humans strike the palms of their hands together repeatedly ► as an expression of strong emotions, including joy and grief

[2KI 11:12](https://ref.ly/2Kgs11:12) · [EZK 6:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek6:11) · [EZK 21:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek21:19) · [EZK 21:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek21:22) · [EZK 22:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek22:13)

Impact \| verb hif, verb nif

to stab, to strike, to strike down, to inflict wounds literally: to strike; hence: \= action by which humans inflict a serious wound on someone else, which is usually fatal

Impact \| verb hif

**Collocation:** נכה חֲלָלִים

to strike down literally: to strike mortally wounded; hence: \= action by which humans inflict a serious wound on someone else, which is usually fatal

[JDG 20:39](https://ref.ly/Judg20:39)

Impact \| verb hif, verb pu'al

to strike, to destroy, to ruin literally: to strike down; hence: \= causative action by which animals, deities and natural forces such as hail affect a plant in such a way that it will no longer bring forth fruit

[EXO 9:25](https://ref.ly/Exod9:25) · [EXO 9:25](https://ref.ly/Exod9:25) · [EXO 9:31](https://ref.ly/Exod9:31) · [EXO 9:32](https://ref.ly/Exod9:32) · [PSA 102:5](https://ref.ly/Ps102:5) · [PSA 105:33](https://ref.ly/Ps105:33) · [JON 4:7](https://ref.ly/Jonah4:7)

Chastise \| verb hif, verb hof \| ≈ נטה יָד

to punish literally: to strike; hence: \= action by which deities inflict punishment on individuals and groups

Conflict \| verb hif

to attack literally: to strike; hence: \= action by which humans initiate a violent confrontation with other humans, either as individuals or groups

Control \| verb hif, verb hof

to defeat literally: to strike; hence: \= action by which humans initiate a violent confrontation with other humans and end up being in full control of them

Dead \| verb hif, verb hof

to kill literally: to strike; hence: \= causative action by which humans, animals, or deities cause other humans or animals to die a violent death

## נֵכֶה (id: 004800000000000)

נֵכֶה
=====

noun m · נכה

to attack meaning unsure; literally: to strike; hence, possibly: \= action by which humans initiate a violent confrontation with other humans, either as individuals or groups

## נסה (id: 004828000000000)

to cause to depart, to lead out, to drive out literally to make (someone) pluck up (their tent pegs); hence: \= causative action by which humans or deities cause a relatively large company of humans, together with their possessions, to depart from a place where they had set up a temporary residence

Move \| verb qal

to march, to move about \= action by which a relatively large company of humans and/or animals move from one place to another, whether with a clear destination in mind or not

Blow \| verb hif

to cause to blow \= causative action by which deities cause a wind to blow

[PSA 78:26](https://ref.ly/Ps78:26)

Space \| verb hif

to remove, to set aside \= causative action by which an object is taken away or removed from its original location

[2KI 4:4](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:4)

[JDG 16:20](https://ref.ly/Judg16:20) · [ISA 52:2](https://ref.ly/Isa52:2)

Unsteady \| verb pi, verb qal ptc.pass, verb nif

to shake, to shake off, to shake out \= causative action by which humans, deities, or forces cause an object to shake in such a way that things covering it fall off

[NEH 5:13](https://ref.ly/Neh5:13) · [NEH 5:13](https://ref.ly/Neh5:13) · [NEH 5:13](https://ref.ly/Neh5:13) · [JOB 38:13](https://ref.ly/Job38:13) · [PSA 109:23](https://ref.ly/Ps109:23)

Move \| verb pi

**Collocation:** נער בַּיָּם

to hurl literally: to shake off (something into the sea); hence: \= causative action by which deities cause objects to fall into the sea

[EXO 14:27](https://ref.ly/Exod14:27) · [PSA 136:15](https://ref.ly/Ps136:15)

Stance \| verb qal

**Collocation:** נער כַּפָּיִם

to shake (one's) hands literally: to shake off (one's) palms; hence: \= action by which humans make shaking movements with their hands in order to ensure that objects or substances that stick to them fall off; ≈ used in a figurative sense to denote someone's unwillingness to possess things that are not rightfully theirs

[ISA 33:15](https://ref.ly/Isa33:15)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Jeremiah 51:38; Isaiah 33:9; Judges 16:20; Isaiah 52:2; Nehemiah 5:13; Job 38:13; Psalms 109:23; Exodus 14:27; Psalms 136:15; Isaiah 33:15

## נפץ (id: 004875000000000)

נפץ
===

נפץ (H5310a · H5310b)

verb · מַפָּץ · מַפֵּץ · נֶפֶץ

Impact \| verb qal, verb pu'al

to break, to crush, to smash, to dash to pieces \= causative action by which humans cause an object to be broken into multiple pieces

[JDG 7:19](https://ref.ly/Judg7:19) · [1KI 5:23](https://ref.ly/1Kgs5:23) · [PSA 2:9](https://ref.ly/Ps2:9) · [PSA 137:9](https://ref.ly/Ps137:9) · [ISA 27:9](https://ref.ly/Isa27:9) · [JER 13:14](https://ref.ly/Jer13:14) · [JER 22:28](https://ref.ly/Jer22:28) · [JER 48:12](https://ref.ly/Jer48:12) · [JER 51:20](https://ref.ly/Jer51:20) · [JER 51:21](https://ref.ly/Jer51:21) · [JER 51:21](https://ref.ly/Jer51:21) · [JER 51:22](https://ref.ly/Jer51:22) · [JER 51:22](https://ref.ly/Jer51:22) · [JER 51:22](https://ref.ly/Jer51:22) · [JER 51:23](https://ref.ly/Jer51:23) · [JER 51:23](https://ref.ly/Jer51:23) · [JER 51:23](https://ref.ly/Jer51:23)

End

to break, to shatter literally: to break; hence: \= causative process by which an event is brought to an end

[DAN 12:7](https://ref.ly/Dan12:7)

Scatter \| verb qal

to spread out, to scatter \= causative process by which a group of humans is caused to divide itself and move into various directions

[GEN 9:19](https://ref.ly/Gen9:19) · [1SA 13:11](https://ref.ly/1Sam13:11) · [ISA 33:3](https://ref.ly/Isa33:3)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Judges 7:19; 1 Kings 5:23; Psalms 2:9; Psalms 137:9; Isaiah 27:9; Jeremiah 13:14; Jeremiah 22:28; Jeremiah 48:12; Jeremiah 51:20; Jeremiah 51:21; Jeremiah 51:22; Jeremiah 51:23; Daniel 12:7; Genesis 9:19; 1 Samuel 13:11; Isaiah 33:3

נפק

Move \| verb pe'al

to come out, to pour out \= process by which a substance flows out of a certain location

[DAN 7:10](https://ref.ly/Dan7:10)

Move \| verb pe'al

go out, come out \= action by which humans leave a certain location

Move \| verb haf'el

to take out \= causative action by which humans remove objects from a certain location

See \| verb pe'al

to appear literally: to come out; hence: \= process by which an object comes into sight

Know \| verb pe'al

to go out, to be issued literally: to come out; hence: \= process by which certain information is made public

## נֶפֶשׁ (id: 004880000000000)

נֶפֶשׁ
======

נֶפֶשׁ (H5315)

noun f · נפשׁ

\| ≈ גַּרְגֶּרֶת · פִּי · רֶגֶל

throat, neck, gullet \= the part of the body connecting the head to the rest of the body and containing the passageways for blood, air, and food; ≈ associated with breathing, appetite, and life and often used metonymically to refer to the entire body and the personality inhabiting it

[NUM 11:6](https://ref.ly/Num11:6)1 · [PSA 69:2](https://ref.ly/Ps69:2) · [PSA 105:18](https://ref.ly/Ps105:18) · [PRO 3:22](https://ref.ly/Prov3:22) · [ISA 5:14](https://ref.ly/Isa5:14) · [ISA 29:8](https://ref.ly/Isa29:8) · [ISA 29:8](https://ref.ly/Isa29:8) · [ISA 32:6](https://ref.ly/Isa32:6) · [JER 4:10](https://ref.ly/Jer4:10) · [JON 2:6](https://ref.ly/Jonah2:6) · [HAB 2:5](https://ref.ly/Hab2:5)2

Air

breath literally: throat, but with focus on the air flowing through it; hence: \= process by which air flows in and out of the body, which shows that a person or animal is alive

[JOB 11:20](https://ref.ly/Job11:20) · [JOB 41:13](https://ref.ly/Job41:13)

Self \| ≈ בֶּטֶן · בָּשָׂר · חַיָּה · כָּבֹוד · לֵב · לֵבָב · מְאֹד · עֶצֶם · רוּחַ \| ≠ בָּשָׂר

life, life principle, soul, self, greed, craving literally: throat, as the part of the body that contains the passageways for blood, air, and food; hence: \= the life principle that animates both humans and animals, turns them into breathing living beings, and functions as the center of their personality, mind, physical and non\-physical desires, courage, emotions, and affections; it is believed to reside in the blood

noun f

Spices

perfume (?) conjectured meaning: \= some kind of airy substance, a scent of some sort

[ISA 3:20](https://ref.ly/Isa3:20)6

1 NUM 11:6 NJPS "gullets" \| Gesenius "Kehle" (cf. Dahood on PSA 105:18\) 2 HAB 2:5 NRSV REB "throat" \| NJPS "maw" 3 2SA 18:13 MT\-K בנפשׁו \| MT\-Q בְנַפְשִׁי 4 JOB 33:28 MT\-K נפשׁי \| MT\-Q נַפְשֹׁו 5 JER 2:24 MT\-K נפשׁו \| MT\-Q נַפְשָׁהּ 6 ISA 3:20 The meaning of בָתֵּי הַנֶּפֶשׁ is controversial: RSV NRSV NIV CEV "perfume" \| NJB "scent" \| NJPS "talismans" \| REB "lockets" \| GNT "magic charms". The commentary of Wildberger, who understand the expression as meaning "houses of souls" should still be considered the most adequate.

Enio R. Mueller; Reinier de Blois

## נֵצַח (id: 004895000000000)

נֵצַח
=====

noun m · נצח

Time

**Collocation:** לָנֶצַח · נֵצַח · עַד־נֵעַח

forever poetic term: \= a long duration of time that is or may seem unending, usually in the future

## נצל (id: 004898000000000)

נצל
===

נצל (H5337 · A5338)

verb · הַצָּלָה

Non\-Whole \| verb hof

remove (violently), to pluck out, to snatch from \= causative action by which humans remove an object from a situation where it could be damaged

[AMO 4:11](https://ref.ly/Amos4:11) · [ZEC 3:2](https://ref.ly/Zech3:2)

Non\-Engage \| verb hif

**Collocation:** נצל בֵּין

to stop, to separate literally: to deliver between (two people); hence: \= causative action by which humans intervene when other humans are fighting

[2SA 14:6](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:6)

Possess \| verb pi

to plunder, to strip \= causative action by which humans remove or carry away valuable goods from people that have been defeated in war

Possess \| verb hif

to take away, to snatch away, to recover \= causative action by which humans or deities remove (other) humans or objects from someone else's possession

## נֵר (id: 004925000000000)

נֵר
===

נֵר (H5216a · H5369)

noun m · מְנֹורָה · נִיר

## נשׁא (id: 004930000000000)

נשׁא
====

נשׁא (H5377 · H5378 · H5383)

verb · מַשָּׁא · מַשּׁוּאָה · נְשִׁי · מַשֶּׁה

Non\-Possess \| verb qal, verb hif

to lend \= action with which a person gives money or something of value to another person with the expectation that it will be paid back or returned, which can become a burden weighing heavily on the borrower

[EXO 22:24](https://ref.ly/Exod22:24) · [DEU 15:2](https://ref.ly/Deut15:2) · [DEU 24:10](https://ref.ly/Deut24:10) · [DEU 24:11](https://ref.ly/Deut24:11) · [1SA 22:2](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:2) · [2KI 4:1](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:1) · [NEH 5:7](https://ref.ly/Neh5:7) · [NEH 5:10](https://ref.ly/Neh5:10) · [NEH 5:11](https://ref.ly/Neh5:11) · [PSA 109:11](https://ref.ly/Ps109:11) · [ISA 24:2](https://ref.ly/Isa24:2) · [ISA 24:2](https://ref.ly/Isa24:2) · [ISA 50:1](https://ref.ly/Isa50:1) · [JER 15:10](https://ref.ly/Jer15:10) · [JER 15:10](https://ref.ly/Jer15:10)

Act \| verb qal

to oblige, to require \= causative action in which a person is forced or made to state a case or perform an action ◄ as if it were owed

[1KI 8:31](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:31) · [2CH 6:22](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:22)

verb · מַשָּׁאֹון

Foolish \| verb nif

to be deceived, to be deluded \= passive action by which a person is fooled or deceived

[ISA 19:13](https://ref.ly/Isa19:13)

Foolish \| verb hif

to deceive, to fool, to outsmart \= action with which someone misleads or deceives another person

[GEN 3:13](https://ref.ly/Gen3:13) · [2KI 18:29](https://ref.ly/2Kgs18:29) · [2KI 19:10](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:10) · [2CH 32:15](https://ref.ly/2Chr32:15) · [PSA 55:16](https://ref.ly/Ps55:16) · [PSA 89:23](https://ref.ly/Ps89:23) · [ISA 36:14](https://ref.ly/Isa36:14) · [ISA 37:10](https://ref.ly/Isa37:10) · [JER 4:10](https://ref.ly/Jer4:10) · [JER 4:10](https://ref.ly/Jer4:10) · [JER 29:8](https://ref.ly/Jer29:8) · [JER 37:9](https://ref.ly/Jer37:9) · [JER 49:16](https://ref.ly/Jer49:16) · [OBA 1:3](https://ref.ly/Obad1:3) · [OBA 1:7](https://ref.ly/Obad1:7)

## נשׁב (id: 004932000000000)

נשׁב
====

נשׁב (H5380)

verb

Blow \| verb qal

to blow \= process by which air moves across a surface or against an object

[ISA 40:7](https://ref.ly/Isa40:7)

Blow \| verb hif

to make to blow \= causative action by which deities cause air to move across a surface or against an object

[PSA 147:18](https://ref.ly/Ps147:18)

Move \| verb hif

to drive away, to chase away \= causative action by which a person moves or drives away another person or animal, perhaps originally by blowing a horn

[GEN 15:11](https://ref.ly/Gen15:11)

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 40:7; Psalms 147:18; Genesis 15:11


## נשׂג (id: 004933000000000)

נשׂג
====

נשׂג (H5381)

verb

Pursue \| verb hif

to overtake, to catch up with \= action by which humans succeed to catch up with other humans after having pursued them

[GEN 31:25](https://ref.ly/Gen31:25) · [GEN 44:4](https://ref.ly/Gen44:4) · [GEN 44:6](https://ref.ly/Gen44:6) · [EXO 14:9](https://ref.ly/Exod14:9) · [EXO 15:9](https://ref.ly/Exod15:9) · [DEU 19:6](https://ref.ly/Deut19:6) · [JOS 2:5](https://ref.ly/Josh2:5) · [1SA 30:8](https://ref.ly/1Sam30:8) · [1SA 30:8](https://ref.ly/1Sam30:8) · [1SA 30:8](https://ref.ly/1Sam30:8) · [2SA 15:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam15:14) · [2KI 25:5](https://ref.ly/2Kgs25:5) · [PSA 7:6](https://ref.ly/Ps7:6) · [PSA 18:38](https://ref.ly/Ps18:38) · [JER 39:5](https://ref.ly/Jer39:5) · [JER 52:8](https://ref.ly/Jer52:8) · [LAM 1:3](https://ref.ly/Lam1:3) · [HOS 2:9](https://ref.ly/Hos2:9)

Happen \| verb hif, verb nif

to catch up with (\= happen) literally: to overtake; hence: \= process by which events that humans have been expecting or dreading finally take place, ◄ as if they had been pursuing them for some time and ultimately caught up with them

[DEU 28:2](https://ref.ly/Deut28:2) · [DEU 28:15](https://ref.ly/Deut28:15) · [DEU 28:45](https://ref.ly/Deut28:45) · [1CH 21:12](https://ref.ly/1Chr21:12) · [JOB 27:20](https://ref.ly/Job27:20) · [JOB 41:18](https://ref.ly/Job41:18) · [PSA 40:13](https://ref.ly/Ps40:13) · [PSA 69:25](https://ref.ly/Ps69:25) · [ISA 35:10](https://ref.ly/Isa35:10) · [ISA 51:11](https://ref.ly/Isa51:11) · [ISA 59:9](https://ref.ly/Isa59:9) · [JER 42:16](https://ref.ly/Jer42:16) · [HOS 10:9](https://ref.ly/Hos10:9) · [MIC 2:6](https://ref.ly/Mic2:6)1 · [ZEC 1:6](https://ref.ly/Zech1:6)

Engage \| verb hif \| ≈ שׁוב

**Collocation:** נשׂג אֹרַח

to regain a path, to reengage literally: to catch up with a path; hence: \= process by which humans reengage with a particular activity

[PRO 2:19](https://ref.ly/Prov2:19)

Quantity \| verb hif

to catch up with (in number) literally: to overtake; hence: \= process by which a repetitive event increases in frequency to the extent that it starts matching the frequency of another event

[GEN 47:9](https://ref.ly/Gen47:9)

Rich \| verb hif

**Collocation:** יָד נשׂג

to afford literally: (one's) hand catches up (with something); hence: \= state in which someone has sufficient resources to carry out a certain task

[LEV 5:11](https://ref.ly/Lev5:11) · [LEV 14:21](https://ref.ly/Lev14:21) · [LEV 14:22](https://ref.ly/Lev14:22) · [LEV 14:30](https://ref.ly/Lev14:30) · [LEV 14:31](https://ref.ly/Lev14:31) · [LEV 14:32](https://ref.ly/Lev14:32) · [LEV 25:26](https://ref.ly/Lev25:26) · [LEV 25:47](https://ref.ly/Lev25:47) · [LEV 25:49](https://ref.ly/Lev25:49) · [LEV 27:8](https://ref.ly/Lev27:8) · [NUM 6:21](https://ref.ly/Num6:21) · [EZK 46:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek46:7)

Time \| verb hif

to catch up with (in time) literally: to overtake; hence: \= process by which a certain event takes up so much time that it extends into the time alotted for the event that should happen next

[LEV 26:5](https://ref.ly/Lev26:5) · [LEV 26:5](https://ref.ly/Lev26:5)

verb

Stance \| verb hif

**Collocation:** נשׂג יָד

to move (one's) hand \= action by which humans cause their hands to move in a certain direction

Birth

Non\-Engage \| verb hif \| ≈ פתח חַרצֻבֹּות רֶשַׁע

**Collocation:** נתר אֲגֻדַּת מֹוטָה

to loosen the cords of the yoke \> to stop oppressing other people literally: to loosen the cords of the yoke; hence: \= action by which humans stop oppressing other people

[ISA 58:6](https://ref.ly/Isa58:6)

Free \| verb hif

**Collocation:** נתר יָד

to give one's hand free play literally: to release (one's) hand; \= action by which a deity lets go of whatever restrains him from acting in a certain way

[JOB 6:9](https://ref.ly/Job6:9)

Free \| verb hif

to free, to release \= action by which humans or deities give freedom to (other) humans that were held in bondage

[PSA 105:20](https://ref.ly/Ps105:20) · [PSA 146:7](https://ref.ly/Ps146:7)

Well \| verb hif

**Collocation:** נתר דֶּרֶךְ תָּמִים

to make (someone's) way blameless literally, possibly: to loosen (somone's) way blameless; hence: \= causative action by which deities help humans to live a blameless life

[2SA 22:33](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:33)

verb

Leap \| verb pi

to jump, to leap, to hop \= action by which certain insects move by jumping from one place to the other

[LEV 11:21](https://ref.ly/Lev11:21)

Unsteady \| verb qal

**Collocation:** לֵב נתר מִמְּקֹומֹו

(one's) heart leaps from its place literally: (one's) heart leaps from its place; hence: \= state in which humans experience a state of strong fear, which results in one's heart beating wildly

[JOB 37:1](https://ref.ly/Job37:1)

Unsteady \| verb hif

to cause to shake literally: to cause (people) to leap; hence: \= causative action by which deities cause humans to experience a state of extreme fear which makes their bodies shake

[HAB 3:6](https://ref.ly/Hab3:6)

verb

Detach

to strip off \= causative action by which someone removes all leaves from the branches of a tree

[DAN 4:11](https://ref.ly/Dan4:11)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 58:6; Job 6:9; Psalms 105:20; Psalms 146:7; 2 Samuel 22:33; Leviticus 11:21; Job 37:1; Habakkuk 3:6; Daniel 4:11


## נֶתֶר (id: 004977000000000)

נֶתֶר
=====

נֶתֶר (H5427)

noun m

Substances \| ≈ בֹּרִית

natron, soda \= sodium carbonate ► used as a dye, medicament, and cleansing agent (AYBC)

[PRO 25:20](https://ref.ly/Prov25:20)1 · [JER 2:22](https://ref.ly/Jer2:22)

1 PRO 25:20 MT HOTTP\-B NIV NJPS \| LXX RSV NJB NRSV REB GNT CEV נֶתֶק "wound"

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Proverbs 25:20; Jeremiah 2:22


## נתשׁ (id: 004978000000000)

נתשׁ
====

נתשׁ (H5428)

verb

Detach \| verb qal, verb hof

to uproot \= causative action by which a plant or pole is pulled out of the ground; ≈ associated with destruction and exile

[JER 45:4](https://ref.ly/Jer45:4) · [EZK 19:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek19:12) · [MIC 5:13](https://ref.ly/Mic5:13)

Non\-Exist \| verb qal, verb nif

to destroy literally: to uproot; hence: \= causative action by which a town or land is destroyed, ◄ like a plant pulled out of the ground

[PSA 9:7](https://ref.ly/Ps9:7) · [JER 31:40](https://ref.ly/Jer31:40)

Dry \| verb nif

to run dry literally: to be uprooted; hence: \= process by which a body of water ceases to flow and vanishes

[JER 18:14](https://ref.ly/Jer18:14)1

End \| verb nif

to be uprooted \> come to an end literally: to be uprooted; hence: \= process by which a state of affairs comes to a violent end

[DAN 11:4](https://ref.ly/Dan11:4)

Move \| verb qal, verb nif

to uproot, to expel literally: to uproot; hence: \= causative action by which deities cause people to leave their land, ◄ like a plant pulled out of the ground

[DEU 29:27](https://ref.ly/Deut29:27) · [1KI 14:15](https://ref.ly/1Kgs14:15) · [2CH 7:20](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:20) · [JER 1:10](https://ref.ly/Jer1:10) · [JER 12:14](https://ref.ly/Jer12:14) · [JER 12:14](https://ref.ly/Jer12:14) · [JER 12:15](https://ref.ly/Jer12:15) · [JER 12:17](https://ref.ly/Jer12:17) · [JER 12:17](https://ref.ly/Jer12:17) · [JER 18:7](https://ref.ly/Jer18:7) · [JER 24:6](https://ref.ly/Jer24:6) · [JER 31:28](https://ref.ly/Jer31:28) · [JER 42:10](https://ref.ly/Jer42:10) · [AMO 9:15](https://ref.ly/Amos9:15)

1 JER 18:14 MT HOTTP\-A \| others emend the text to ינשׁתו but the same meaning can be obtained by interpreting the MT as a figurative extension of meaning of נתשׁ.

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Jeremiah 45:4; Ezekiel 19:12; Micah 5:13; Psalms 9:7; Jeremiah 31:40; Jeremiah 18:14; Daniel 11:4; Deuteronomy 29:27; 1 Kings 14:15; 2 Chronicles 7:20; Jeremiah 1:10; Jeremiah 12:14; Jeremiah 12:15; Jeremiah 12:17; Jeremiah 18:7; Jeremiah 24:6; Jeremiah 31:28; Jeremiah 42:10; Amos 9:15
